The functions are similar to the ones in the class-based API, but they return Effects instead of Promises, with some error handling. Over time, the Effect API might be expanded to include more features. Please open an issue if you have any requests for how we can make the API more ergonomic or â€œEffectful.â€"]}],"\n",["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-6 x:leading-7","children":["The test utils mentioned in the ",["$","$Ld",null,{"href":"/guides/testing-sidetrack","className":"x:focus-visible:nextra-focus x:text-primary-600 x:underline x:hover:no-underline x:decoration-from-font x:[text-underline-position:from-font]","children":"Testing Sidetrack"}]," section can also be found under the ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"testUtils"}]," key in the sidetrack service.
